<script type="text/javascript">
        var urlAvancee='&zone1=titreRAs&val1=&op1=AND&zone2=auteurs&val2=&op2=AND&zone3=etabSoutenances&val3=&op3=AND&zone4=dateSoutenance&val4a=&val4b=&type=';

        $(document).ready(function($) {

            
            $('#receive').append('<div class="u_date">'+'De '+1965+' à '+2020+'</div>');
            

            document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML="";
            var facetteOk = "";
            $('.checkers').each(function(index) {
                var id = '.u_'+$(this).attr('id');
                var test = $(this).attr('id')+'_lbl';
                var testlabel = '#'+test;
                var control=0;

                if($(this).is(':checked') && $('#receive div'+id).length == 0) {
                    var label = $(testlabel).html();
                    if (test.indexOf('etablissement')>=0) {
                        label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                        control++;
                    }
                    if (test.indexOf('langueThese')>=0) {
                        label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                        control++;
                    }
                    if (test.indexOf('oaiSetSpec')>=0) {
                        label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                        control++;
                    }
                    if (test.indexOf('role')>=0) {
                        label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                        control++;
                        }
                    if (control!=0) {
                        $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_'+$(this).attr('id')+'">'+label+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
                    } else if (control==0) {
                        $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_'+$(this).attr('id')+'">'+$(this).val()+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
                    }
                    facetteOk+=$(this).attr('id').substring(0,$(this).attr('id').indexOf('_'))+"="+$(this).val()+";";
                    $('div.showhide,h2').show();
               }

            });
            document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML=facetteOk;

            $('.checkers').bind('click', function() {
                var id = '.u_'+$(this).attr('id');
                var test = $(this).attr('id')+'_lbl';
                var testlabel = '#'+test;
                var control=0;
                if($(this).is(':checked')) {
                    if($('#receive div'+id).length == 0) {
                        $('div.showhide,h2').show();

                        var label = $(testlabel).html();
                        if (test.indexOf('etablissement')>=0) {
                            label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                            control++;
                        }
                        if (test.indexOf('langueThese')>=0) {
                            label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                            control++;
                        }
                        if (test.indexOf('oaiSetSpec')>=0) {
                            label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                            control++;
                        }
                        if (test.indexOf('role')>=0) {
                            label = label.substring(0,label.indexOf('('));
                            control++;
                        }
                        if (control!=0) {
                            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_'+$(this).attr('id')+'">'+label+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
                        } else if (control==0) {
                            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_'+$(this).attr('id')+'">'+$(this).val()+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    $(id).remove();
                }
            });

            $('.delete').live('click',function() {
                var id = $(this).parent().attr('class').split('_');
                $('#'+id[1]+"_"+id[2]).attr('checked', false);
                if (id[1].toString() != 'rech'){
                    checkBox(id[1], $('#'+id[1]+"_"+id[2]).attr('value'));
                } else if (id[1].toString() == 'rech'){
                    $('#q').val(" ");
                    createCookie("q", " ", 15);
                    facettes_checked_list=document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML;
                    window.location=  '?q=:*:*'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+facettes_checked_list+'&start=0'+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
                }
                $(this).parent().remove();
            });
        });
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    function rechercheAvancee() {
        videRecherches();
        $('#rechAvancee2').toggle();
        if ($('#rechAvancee2').is(':visible')) {
            $('#rechAvancee2 :input').removeAttr('disabled');
            $('#rech, #autoCs').hide();
            $('#libLienRechAv').text("Recherche simple");
            
        }
        else {
            $('#rechAvancee2 :input').attr('disabled', true);
            $('#rech, #autoCs').show();
            $('#libLienRechAv').text("Recherche avancée");
        }
    }

    function videRecherches() {
        $('#zone1').val("titreRAs");
        $('#val1').val("");
        $('#op1').val("AND");
        $('#zone2').val("auteurs");
        $('#val2').val("");
        $('#op2').val("AND");
        $('#zone3').val("etabSoutenances");
        $('#val3').val("");
        $('#op3').val("AND");
        $('#zone4').val("dateSoutenance");
        $('#q').val("");
        $('#val4a').val("");
        $('#val4b').val("");
    }

    $(function() {

        if (!$('#rechAvancee2').is(':visible')) {
            $('#rechAvancee2 :input').attr('disabled', true);
        }

        $( "#val4a" ).datepicker({
            defaultDate: "+1w",
            changeMonth: true,
            changeYear: true,
            numberOfMonths: 3,
            onClose: function( selectedDate ) {
                $( "#val4a" ).datepicker( "option", "minDate", selectedDate );
            }
        });
        
        $.datepicker.regional['fr'] = {clearText: 'Effacer', clearStatus: '',
                closeText: 'Fermer', closeStatus: 'Fermer sans modifier',
                prevText: '<Préc', prevStatus: 'Voir le mois précédent',

                currentText: 'Courant', currentStatus: 'Voir le mois courant',

                monthNamesShort: ['Jan','Fév','Mar','Avr','Mai','Jun','Jul','Aoû','Sep','Oct','Nov','Déc'],
                monthStatus: 'Voir un autre mois', yearStatus: 'Voir un autre année',
                weekHeader: 'Sm', weekStatus: '',
                dayNames: ['Dimanche','Lundi','Mardi','Mercredi','Jeudi','Vendredi','Samedi'],
                dayNamesShort: ['Dim','Lun','Mar','Mer','Jeu','Ven','Sam'],
                dayNamesMin: ['Di','Lu','Ma','Me','Je','Ve','Sa'],
                dayStatus: 'Utiliser DD comme premier jour de la semaine', dateStatus: 'Choisir le DD, MM d',
                dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy', firstDay: 0, 
                initStatus: 'Choisir la date', isRTL: false};
        $.datepicker.setDefaults($.datepicker.regional['fr']);
        
        $( "#val4b" ).datepicker({
            defaultDate: "+1w",
            changeMonth: true,

    });

<script type="text/javascript">

    //Changement de périmètre
    function changePeri(peri) {
        // Cas d'une autre page (détail), on essaie de prendre le paramètre q
        if (!$('#q').hasClass('placeholder') && jQuery.trim($('#q').val())!="") {
            window.location="/"+peri+"?q="+jQuery.trim($('#q').val());
        } else {
            window.location="/"+peri;
        }
    }

    //Affiche/cache l'encart recherche avancée
    function affichRechercheAvancee() {
        $('#rechercheAvancee').toggle();
        return false;
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var facettes_checked_list="";

    function open_facette(showHideDiv, switchImgTag) {
        var ele = document.getElementById(showHideDiv);
        var imageEle = document.getElementById(switchImgTag);
        if (ele.style.display == "block") {
            ele.style.display = "none";
            imageEle.innerHTML = '<img src="/img/add_mini.gif">';
        } else {
            ele.style.display = "block";
            imageEle.innerHTML = '<img src="/img/remove_mini.gif">';
        }
    }

    // Fonction appelée pour l'export de la liste de résultat
    function exportResultat(url) {
        window.location=url.replace(/[\s|\+]/g,"%2B").replace(/é/g,"%E9")
            .replace(/è/g,"%E8").replace(/ê/g,"%EA").replace(/ç/g,"%E7").replace(/à/g,"%E0");
    }

    function doValider(idForm) {
        var myAjax = new Ajax.Request(
                'Compte?'+$(idForm).serialize(),
                {method: 'post', onComplete: doValiderOk}
        );
    }

    function doValiderOk(originalRequest) {
        var docXml = Sarissa.getDomDocument();
        docXml = (new DOMParser()).parseFromString(originalRequest.responseText, "text/xml");
        docXml.setProperty("SelectionLanguage", "XPath");
        var retour =  docXml.documentElement.selectSingleNode("//@val");

        if (retour.value.include("1"))
            $('sMsg').innerHTML ="La mise à jour a été effectuée";
        else
            $('sMsg').innerHTML ="Une erreur innattendue s'est produite lors de la mise à jour";

        $('addRecherche').hide()
        $('addRechercheOk').show();
    }

    function doAnnulerModale(idDiv) {
      $(idDiv,'fenetreModale').invoke('hide');
    }

    function saveRecherche(url) {
        $('addRecherche','fenetreModale').invoke('show');
        $('txtUrl').setValue(url);
        $('txtNbRes').setValue($('sNbRes').innerHTML);
    }

    function Remplace(expr,a,b) {
        var i=0
        while (i!=-1) {
            i=expr.indexOf(a,i);
            if (i>=0) {
                expr=expr.substring(0,i)+b+expr.substring(i+a.length);
                i+=b.length;
            }
        }
        return expr
    }

    function checkBox(nom, valeur) {

        valeur = valeur.replace("&","%26");
        facettes_checked_list=document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML;

        if(facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom+"="+valeur+";") == -1) {
            valeur = valeur.replace(/\''/g,"\\\"");
            facettes_checked_list = facettes_checked_list +nom+'='+valeur+";";
        } else {
            if(facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom+"="+valeur+";") != -1){
                var lg = facettes_checked_list.length;
                facettes_checked_list=Remplace(facettes_checked_list,nom+'='+valeur+";","");
            }
        }
        facettes_checked_list=facettes_checked_list.replace("&amp;","%26");
        window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+facettes_checked_list+'&start=0'+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
    }

    function checkboxoverlays(nom, valeur) {
        valeur = valeur.replace("&","%26");
        facettes_checked_list=document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML;

        if(facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom+"="+valeur+";") == -1) {
            valeur = valeur.replace(/\''/g,"\\\""); 
            facettes_checked_list = facettes_checked_list +nom+'='+valeur+";";
        } else {
            if(facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom+"="+valeur+";") != -1){
                var lg = facettes_checked_list.length;
                facettes_checked_list=Remplace(facettes_checked_list,nom+'='+valeur+";","");
            }
        }

        facettes_checked_list=facettes_checked_list.replace("&amp;","%26");
        $("#facetsvalues").html(facettes_checked_list);
        // window.location=  '?q=finance marché'+'&checkedfacets='+facettes_checked_list+'&start=0'+'&status='+document.getElementById('statusbox').checked+'&access='+document.getElementById('accessbox').checked;
    }

    function encode(startpage) {
        var selObj =  document.getElementById('selectsort');
        var selIndex = selObj.selectedIndex;
        window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+startpage+'&sort='+selObj.options[selIndex].value+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
    }

    function changesortoption(t){
        var selObj =  t;
        var selIndex = t.selectedIndex;
        window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+'&start=0'+'&sort='+selObj.options[selIndex].value+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
    }

    function callsolr(){
        window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+$("#facetsvalues").html()+'&start=0'+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+urlAvancee;
        return false;
    }

    function checkboxAlloverlays(theElement,overlay) {
        var theForm = theElement.form, z = 0;

        for(z=0; z<theForm.length;z++){
            if(theForm[z].type == 'checkbox'  && theForm[z].name != 'checkall' && theForm[z].name.indexOf(overlay, 0) >= 0) {
                theForm[z].checked = theElement.checked;
                $('#'+theForm[z].id).change();
            }
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function() {

    $(".personne_main").scrollable({vertical: false}).navigator(".personne_roles");
    $(".personne_scrollable").scrollable({ vertical: true, mousewheel: true }).navigator(".personne_navi");

    jQuery.expr[':'].Contains = function(li,i,m) {
        return (li.textContent || li.innerText || "").toUpperCase().indexOf(m[3].toUpperCase())>=0;
    };

    function listFilter(input, list) {
        $(input).change( function () {
            }).keyup( function () {
                $(this).change();
                });

        $(input).change( function () {
            var filter = $(this).val();
            if (filter) {
                $(list).find("li:not(:Contains(" + filter + "))").hide();
                $(list).find("li:Contains(" + filter + ")").show();
            } else {
                $(list).find("li").show();
            }
            });
        }
        listFilter("#searchInput0",".wrapper_global");
        listFilter("#searchInput1",".wrapper_global");
        listFilter("#searchInput2",".wrapper_global");
        listFilter("#searchInput3",".wrapper_global");
        listFilter("#searchInput4",".wrapper_global");
        listFilter("#searchInput5",".wrapper_global");

        $("#partager").tooltip({ delay:30, offset: [5,0], effect: 'slide'});
        $("#exporter").tooltip({ delay:30, offset: [5,20], effect: 'slide'});
        $("#abonner").tooltip({ delay:30, offset: [5,0], effect: 'slide'});

        $('input[placeholder]').placeholder();

        $("img[rel]").overlay({
            mask: {
                color: '#000',
                loadSpeed: 200,
                opacity: 0.8
            },
            onClose: function() {
                callsolr(); },
            checkboxoverlays: function(nom, valeur) {
                valeur = valeur.replace("&","%26");
                facettes_checked_list=$("#facetsvalues").html();
                if (facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom+"="+valeur) == -1) {
                    facettes_checked_list = facettes_checked_list +";"+nom+'='+valeur;
                } else {
                    if (facettes_checked_list.indexOf(nom) != -1) {
                        var lg = facettes_checked_list.length;
                        facettes_checked_list=Remplace(facettes_checked_list,nom+'='+valeur+";","");
                        if (lg == facettes_checked_list.length) {
                            facettes_checked_list=Remplace(facettes_checked_list,";"+nom+'='+valeur,"");
                        }
                    }
                }
                $("#facetsvalues").html(facettes_checked_list); }
            }
        );

        var annee0 = 1965;
        var annee1 = 2020;
        if (annee0==1965) {
            annee0='avant2010';
        }
        if (annee1==2030) {
            annee1="apres2020";
        }

        $( "#slider" ).slider({
            range: true,
            min: 2009,
            max: 2021,
            values: [ 1965, 2020 ],
            slide: function( event, ui ) {

                annee0 = ui.values[ 0 ];
                annee1 = ui.values[ 1 ];
                if (ui.values[ 0 ]==2009) {
                    ui.values[ 0 ]="1965";
                    annee0='avant2010';
                }
                if (ui.values[ 1 ]==2021) {
                    ui.values[ 1 ]="2030";
                    annee1='apres2020';
                }

                // Curseur max ne peut pas aller au min
                if (ui.values[ 1 ]==2009){
                    ui.values[ 1 ]="2010";
                    annee1=ui.values[ 1 ];
                }

                $( "#dates" ).html( 'De ' + annee0 + ' à ' + annee1 );

                var id = '.u_date';
                var iddate = 'u_date';
                if($('#receive div'+id).length == 0) {
                    $('div.showhide,h2').show();
                    
                    $('#receive').append('<div class="'+iddate+'">'+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+'</div>');
                    

                    facettes_checked_list=document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML;
                    facettes_checked_list = facettes_checked_list +id+'='+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+";";
                } else {
                    $(id).remove();
                    
                    $('#receive').append('<div class="'+iddate+'">'+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+'</div>');
                    
                    facettes_checked_list=document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML;
                    facettes_checked_list = facettes_checked_list +id+'='+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+";";
                }

                $("#datedebsoutenance").html(ui.values[ 0 ]);
                $("#datefinsoutenance").html(ui.values[ 1 ]);
            },
            stop: function( event, ui ) {
                annee0 = ui.values[ 0 ];
                annee1 = ui.values[ 1 ];
                if (ui.values[ 0 ]==2009){
                    ui.values[ 0 ]="1965";
                    annee0='avant2010';
                }
                if (ui.values[ 1 ]==2021){
                    ui.values[ 1 ]="2030";
                    annee1='apres2020';
                }
                //Curseur max ne peut pas aller au min
                if (ui.values[ 1 ]==2009){
                    ui.values[ 1 ]="2010";
                    annee1=ui.values[ 1 ];
                }
                //ACT pour la CGE
                window.location="/?q=finance march\u00E9&fq=dateSoutenance:["+ui.values[ 0 ]+"-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B"+ui.values[ 1 ]+"-12-31T23:59:59Z]"+'&checkedfacets='+$("#facetsvalues").html()+'&start=0'+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
            }
        });

        $( "#dates" ).html( 'De ' + annee0 + ' à ' + annee1 );

        var id = '.u_date';
        var iddate = 'u_date';
        if ($('#receive div'+id).length == 0) {
            $('div.showhide,h2').show();
            
            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+iddate+'">'+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+'</div>');
            
        } else {
            $(id).remove();
            
            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+iddate+'">'+'De '+annee0+' à '+annee1+'</div>');
            
        }

        $(".signin").click(function() {
            $("fieldset#signin_menu").toggle();
            $(".signin").toggleClass("menu-open");
        });

        $("fieldset#signin_menu").mouseup(function() {
            return false
        });

        $(document).mouseup(function(e) {
            if($(e.target).parent("a.signin").length==0) {
                $(".signin").removeClass("menu-open");
                $("fieldset#signin_menu").hide();
            }
        });
        $('#q').clearableTextField();
        $('#q').val("finance marché");

        if (jQuery.trim($('#q').val())!="") {
            trigger($('#q'));
            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_rech'+'">'+document.getElementById('q').value+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
        }
        // init le cookie aussi pr que la valeur reste !!!
        createCookie("q", "finance march\u00E9", 15);

        $( "#q" ).autocomplete(
                {source: '/Recherche?autoc=true'},
                {
                    select: function( event, ui ) {
                        this.value= "\""+ui.item.value+"\"";
                        return false;
                    }
                }
                )
                .data( "autocomplete" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
                    return $( "<li></li>" )
                        .data( "item.autocomplete", item )
                        .append( "<a>" + item.label + " <i>[" + item.type + "]</i></a>" )
                        .appendTo( ul );
                };

        $('#btnRech').bind('click', function() {
            createCookie("q", "finance march\u00E9", 15);
            $('#receive').append('<div class="'+'u_rech'+'">'+document.getElementById('q').value+'<a class="delete">x</a></div>');
            window.location= '/?q='+document.getElementById('q').value+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
            return false;
        });

    });//fin ready

function handleChangeAccess(cb) {
    if (cb.checked){
        document.getElementById('access').value = 'accessible:oui';
    } else {
        document.getElementById('access').value = '';
    }
    window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
}

function handleChangeStatus(cb) {
    if (cb.checked) {
        document.getElementById('status').value = 'status:soutenue';
    } else {
        document.getElementById('status').value = '';
    }
    window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
}

        document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value = 'oui';

        document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value = '';

    window.location=  '?q=finance march\u00E9'+'&fq=dateSoutenance:['+$("#datedebsoutenance").html()+'-01-01T23:59:59Z%2BTO%2B'+$("#datefinsoutenance").html()+'-12-31T23:59:59Z]'+'&checkedfacets='+document.getElementById('facetsvalues').innerHTML+'&status='+document.getElementById('status').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&access='+document.getElementById('access').value+'&prevision='+document.getElementById('prevision').value+'&filtrepersonne='+document.getElementById('filtrepersonne').value+urlAvancee;
}

}

    function createCookie(name, value, days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
        }
        else expires = "";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + encodeURIComponent(value) + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function readCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }

    //Lien activer/desactiver autocompletion
    function autoC(rep){
        //Si desactive autocomplete
        if (rep=="non") {
            $('#autoCO').hide();
            $('#autoCN').show();
            createCookie("autoC", rep, 15);
            $( "#q" ).autocomplete({ disabled: true });
        }
        else { //sinon
            $('#autoCN').hide();
            $('#autoCO').show();
            createCookie("autoC", rep, 15);
            $( "#q" ).autocomplete({ disabled: false });
        }
    }

    //Lecture cookie pour activer/desactiver autocompletion
    $(document).ready(function($) {
        var cookie = readCookie("autoC");
        var rep = cookie ? cookie : "oui";
        autoC(rep);
    });
